module target(oe, clk, AD, cBE, Frame, TRDY, IRDY, DEVSEL, Reset);
    

input[3:0] cBE, Frame, IRDY, Reset, oe;
output reg [1:0] TRDY, DEVSEL;
inout [31:0] AD ;
reg [31:0] buffer [3:0];
reg [31:0] address ;

always @(posedge clk)
begin
if (~Frame)
begin
	assign address = AD ;
	if ( address == 0 || address == 1 || address == 2 || address ==3)
	begin
		@(negedge clk) 
			DEVSEL <= 0;
			TRDY <= 0;
			if(cBE == 0010 &&  ~TRDY)
				begin
					 assign AD = oe?buffer [address] : 32'bz;
				end
	end
   
end
end
endmodule
module ClockGen (clk);
output clk;
reg clk;
initial
clk = 0;
always
#5 clk = ~clk;
endmodule

module target(oe, clk, AD, cBE, Frame, TRDY, IRDY, DEVSEL, Reset);
    

input[3:0] cBE, Frame, IRDY, Reset, oe;
output reg [1:0] TRDY, DEVSEL;
inout [31:0] AD ;
reg [31:0] buffer [3:0];
reg [31:0] address ;

always @(posedge clk)
begin
if (~Frame)
begin
	assign address = AD ;
	if ( address == 0 || address == 1 || address == 2 || address ==3)
	begin
		@(negedge clk) 
			DEVSEL <= 0;
			TRDY <= 0;
			if(cBE == 0010 &&  ~TRDY)
				begin
					 assign AD = oe?buffer [address] : 32'bz;
				end
	end
   
end
end
endmodule
module ClockGen (clk);
output clk;
reg clk;
initial
clk = 0;
always
#5 clk = ~clk;
endmodule
def edit_product(request, id):
    edit_product = Product.objects.get(pk=id)
    print(edit_product.name)
    print("---------")
    if request.method == 'POST':
        edit_product.name=request.POST['name']
        edit_product.category=request.POST['category']
        edit_product.description=request.POST['descrription']
        edit_product.price=request.POST['price']
        edit_product.quantity=request.POST['quantity']
        edit_product.img=request.POST['img']
        edit_product.offer=request.POST['offer']
        edit_product.save()
        return redirect('/')

module target(oe, clk, AD, cBE, Frame, TRDY, IRDY, DEVSEL, Reset);
    

input[3:0] cBE, Frame, IRDY, Reset, oe;
output reg [1:0] TRDY, DEVSEL;
inout [31:0] AD ;
reg [31:0] buffer [3:0];
reg [31:0] address ;

always @(posedge clk)
begin
if (~Frame)
begin
	assign address = AD ;
	if ( address == 0 || address == 1 || address == 2 || address ==3)
	begin
		@(negedge clk) 
			DEVSEL <= 0;
			TRDY <= 0;
			if(cBE == 0010 &&  ~TRDY)
				begin
					 assign AD = oe?buffer [address] : 32'bz;
				end
	end
   
end
end
endmodule
module ClockGen (clk);
output clk;
reg clk;
initial
clk = 0;
always
#5 clk = ~clk;
endmodule
def edit_product(request, id):
    edit_product = Product.objects.get(pk=id)
    print(edit_product.name)
    print("---------")
    if request.method == 'POST':
        edit_product.name=request.POST['name']
        edit_product.category=request.POST['category']
        edit_product.description=request.POST['descrription']
        edit_product.price=request.POST['price']
        edit_product.quantity=request.POST['quantity']
        edit_product.img=request.POST['img']
        edit_product.offer=request.POST['offer']
        edit_product.save()
        return redirect('/')

module target(oe, clk, AD, cBE, Frame, TRDY, IRDY, DEVSEL, Reset);
    

input[3:0] cBE, Frame, IRDY, Reset, oe;
output reg [1:0] TRDY, DEVSEL;
inout [31:0] AD ;
reg [31:0] buffer [3:0];
reg [31:0] address ;

always @(posedge clk)
begin
if (~Frame)
begin
	assign address = AD ;
	if ( address == 0 || address == 1 || address == 2 || address ==3)
	begin
		@(negedge clk) 
			DEVSEL <= 0;
			TRDY <= 0;
			if(cBE == 0010 &&  ~TRDY)
				begin
					 assign AD = oe?buffer [address] : 32'bz;
				end
	end
   
end
end
endmodule
module ClockGen (clk);
output clk;
reg clk;
initial
clk = 0;
always
#5 clk = ~clk;
endmodule
def edit_product(request, id):
    edit_product = Product.objects.get(pk=id)
    print(edit_product.name)
    print("---------")
    if request.method == 'POST':
        edit_product.name=request.POST['name']
        edit_product.category=request.POST['category']
        edit_product.description=request.POST['descrription']
        edit_product.price=request.POST['price']
        edit_product.quantity=request.POST['quantity']
        edit_product.img=request.POST['img']
        edit_product.offer=request.POST['offer']
        edit_product.save()
        return redirect('/')

module target(oe, clk, AD, cBE, Frame, TRDY, IRDY, DEVSEL, Reset);
    

input[3:0] cBE, Frame, IRDY, Reset, oe;
output reg [1:0] TRDY, DEVSEL;
inout [31:0] AD ;
reg [31:0] buffer [3:0];
reg [31:0] address ;

always @(posedge clk)
begin
if (~Frame)
begin
	assign address = AD ;
	if ( address == 0 || address == 1 || address == 2 || address ==3)
	begin
		@(negedge clk) 
			DEVSEL <= 0;
			TRDY <= 0;
			if(cBE == 0010 &&  ~TRDY)
				begin
					 assign AD = oe?buffer [address] : 32'bz;
				end
	end
   
end
end
endmodule
module ClockGen (clk);
output clk;
reg clk;
initial
clk = 0;
always
#5 clk = ~clk;
endmodule

module target(oe, clk, AD, cBE, Frame, TRDY, IRDY, DEVSEL, Reset);
    

input[3:0] cBE, Frame, IRDY, Reset, oe;
output reg [1:0] TRDY, DEVSEL;
inout [31:0] AD ;
reg [31:0] buffer [3:0];
reg [31:0] address ;

always @(posedge clk)
begin
if (~Frame)
begin
	assign address = AD ;
	if ( address == 0 || address == 1 || address == 2 || address ==3)
	begin
		@(negedge clk) 
			DEVSEL <= 0;
			TRDY <= 0;
			if(cBE == 0010 &&  ~TRDY)
				begin
					 assign AD = oe?buffer [address] : 32'bz;
				end
	end
   
end
end
endmodule
module ClockGen (clk);
output clk;
reg clk;
initial
clk = 0;
always
#5 clk = ~clk;
endmodule

module target(oe, clk, AD, cBE, Frame, TRDY, IRDY, DEVSEL, Reset);
    

input[3:0] cBE, Frame, IRDY, Reset, oe;
output reg [1:0] TRDY, DEVSEL;
inout [31:0] AD ;
reg [31:0] buffer [3:0];
reg [31:0] address ;

always @(posedge clk)
begin
if (~Frame)
begin
	assign address = AD ;
	if ( address == 0 || address == 1 || address == 2 || address ==3)
	begin
		@(negedge clk) 
			DEVSEL <= 0;
			TRDY <= 0;
			if(cBE == 0010 &&  ~TRDY)
				begin
					 assign AD = oe?buffer [address] : 32'bz;
				end
	end
   
end
end
endmodule
module ClockGen (clk);
output clk;
reg clk;
initial
clk = 0;
always
#5 clk = ~clk;
endmodule

module target(oe, clk, AD, cBE, Frame, TRDY, IRDY, DEVSEL, Reset);
    

input[3:0] cBE, Frame, IRDY, Reset, oe;
output reg [1:0] TRDY, DEVSEL;
inout [31:0] AD ;
reg [31:0] buffer [3:0];
reg [31:0] address ;

always @(posedge clk)
begin
if (~Frame)
begin
	assign address = AD ;
	if ( address == 0 || address == 1 || address == 2 || address ==3)
	begin
		@(negedge clk) 
			DEVSEL <= 0;
			TRDY <= 0;
			if(cBE == 0010 &&  ~TRDY)
				begin
					 assign AD = oe?buffer [address] : 32'bz;
				end
	end
   
end
end
endmodule
module ClockGen (clk);
output clk;
reg clk;
initial
clk = 0;
always
#5 clk = ~clk;
endmodule

module target(oe, clk, AD, cBE, Frame, TRDY, IRDY, DEVSEL, Reset);
    

input[3:0] cBE, Frame, IRDY, Reset, oe;
output reg [1:0] TRDY, DEVSEL;
inout [31:0] AD ;
reg [31:0] buffer [3:0];
reg [31:0] address ;

always @(posedge clk)
begin
if (~Frame)
begin
	assign address = AD ;
	if ( address == 0 || address == 1 || address == 2 || address ==3)
	begin
		@(negedge clk) 
			DEVSEL <= 0;
			TRDY <= 0;
			if(cBE == 0010 &&  ~TRDY)
				begin
					 assign AD = oe?buffer [address] : 32'bz;
				end
	end
   
end
end
endmodule
module ClockGen (clk);
output clk;
reg clk;
initial
clk = 0;
always
#5 clk = ~clk;
endmodule
def edit_product(request, id):
    edit_product = Product.objects.get(pk=id)
    print(edit_product.name)
    print("---------")
    if request.method == 'POST':
        edit_product.name=request.POST['name']
        edit_product.category=request.POST['category']
        edit_product.description=request.POST['descrription']
        edit_product.price=request.POST['price']
        edit_product.quantity=request.POST['quantity']
        edit_product.img=request.POST['img']
        edit_product.offer=request.POST['offer']
        edit_product.save()
        return redirect('/')

module target(oe, clk, AD, cBE, Frame, TRDY, IRDY, DEVSEL, Reset);
    

input[3:0] cBE, Frame, IRDY, Reset, oe;
output reg [1:0] TRDY, DEVSEL;
inout [31:0] AD ;
reg [31:0] buffer [3:0];
reg [31:0] address ;

always @(posedge clk)
begin
if (~Frame)
begin
	assign address = AD ;
	if ( address == 0 || address == 1 || address == 2 || address ==3)
	begin
		@(negedge clk) 
			DEVSEL <= 0;
			TRDY <= 0;
			if(cBE == 0010 &&  ~TRDY)
				begin
					 assign AD = oe?buffer [address] : 32'bz;
				end
	end
   
end
end
endmodule
module ClockGen (clk);
output clk;
reg clk;
initial
clk = 0;
always
#5 clk = ~clk;
endmodule
def edit_product(request, id):
    edit_product = Product.objects.get(pk=id)
    print(edit_product.name)
    print("---------")
    if request.method == 'POST':
        edit_product.name=request.POST['name']
        edit_product.category=request.POST['category']
        edit_product.description=request.POST['descrription']
        edit_product.price=request.POST['price']
        edit_product.quantity=request.POST['quantity']
        edit_product.img=request.POST['img']
        edit_product.offer=request.POST['offer']
        edit_product.save()
        return redirect('/')

module target(oe, clk, AD, cBE, Frame, TRDY, IRDY, DEVSEL, Reset);
    

input[3:0] cBE, Frame, IRDY, Reset, oe;
output reg [1:0] TRDY, DEVSEL;
inout [31:0] AD ;
reg [31:0] buffer [3:0];
reg [31:0] address ;

always @(posedge clk)
begin
if (~Frame)
begin
	assign address = AD ;
	if ( address == 0 || address == 1 || address == 2 || address ==3)
	begin
		@(negedge clk) 
			DEVSEL <= 0;
			TRDY <= 0;
			if(cBE == 0010 &&  ~TRDY)
				begin
					 assign AD = oe?buffer [address] : 32'bz;
				end
	end
   
end
end
endmodule
module ClockGen (clk);
output clk;
reg clk;
initial
clk = 0;
always
#5 clk = ~clk;
endmodule
def edit_product(request, id):
    edit_product = Product.objects.get(pk=id)
    print(edit_product.name)
    print("---------")
    if request.method == 'POST':
        edit_product.name=request.POST['name']
        edit_product.category=request.POST['category']
        edit_product.description=request.POST['descrription']
        edit_product.price=request.POST['price']
        edit_product.quantity=request.POST['quantity']
        edit_product.img=request.POST['img']
        edit_product.offer=request.POST['offer']
        edit_product.save()
        return redirect('/')

module target(oe, clk, AD, cBE, Frame, TRDY, IRDY, DEVSEL, Reset);
    

input[3:0] cBE, Frame, IRDY, Reset, oe;
output reg [1:0] TRDY, DEVSEL;
inout [31:0] AD ;
reg [31:0] buffer [3:0];
reg [31:0] address ;

always @(posedge clk)
begin
if (~Frame)
begin
	assign address = AD ;
	if ( address == 0 || address == 1 || address == 2 || address ==3)
	begin
		@(negedge clk) 
			DEVSEL <= 0;
			TRDY <= 0;
			if(cBE == 0010 &&  ~TRDY)
				begin
					 assign AD = oe?buffer [address] : 32'bz;
				end
	end
   
end
end
endmodule
module ClockGen (clk);
output clk;
reg clk;
initial
clk = 0;
always
#5 clk = ~clk;
endmodule

        <div id="contact" class="container">
          <section class="bar">
            <div class="row">
              <div class="col-md-12">
                <div class="heading">
                  <h2>We are here to help you</h2>
